# Simple Icon Badges

All 1760 free SVG icons from [Simple Icons](https://simpleicons.org/) applied to [Shields.io](https://shields.io/) badges for the Markdown file.

## How to use

Copy the appropriate `<img>` element and paste it in your Markdown file (e.g., `README.md`).

### Styles you can use (?style=)

- plastic
- flat
- flat-square
- social
- for-the-badge
